    [Project2].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project2].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project2].[Name] AS [Name], 
    [Project2].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
    [Project2].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
    [Project2].[C2] AS [C2], 
    [Project2].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project2].[Description] AS [Description], 
    [Project2].[Name1] AS [Name1], 
    [Project2].[CreateDateTime1] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
    [Project2].[IsDeleted1] AS [IsDeleted1]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Description] AS [Description], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
        [Join1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C2] ASC

            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C2] ASC

    [Project2].[IsDeleted1] AS [IsDeleted1]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Description] AS [Description], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
        [Join1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C2] ASC

    [Project2].[Name1] AS [Name1], 
    [Project2].[CreateDateTime1] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
    [Project2].[IsDeleted1] AS [IsDeleted1]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1],

        [Join1].[Description] AS [Description], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
        [Join1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C2] ASC

    [Project2].[CreateDateTime1] AS [CreateDateTime1],

        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1],

        [Join1].[Description] AS [Description], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1],

        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]

            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]

    [Project2].[Name] AS [Name],

    [Project2].[Name1] AS [Name1], 
    [Project2].[CreateDateTime1] AS [CreateDateTime1],

    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1],

        [Join1].[Description] AS [Description], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
        [Join1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]

        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1],

        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
        [Join1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]

        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1],

        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id],

            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]

            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]

2019-09-04 18:21:27,586 [10] DEBUG ZSZ.Service.MyContext - EF开始执行sql语句SELECT 
    [Project2].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project2].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project2].[Name] AS [Name], 
    [Project2].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
    [Project2].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
    [Project2].[C2] AS [C2], 
    [Project2].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project2].[Description] AS [Description], 
    [Project2].[Name1] AS [Name1], 
    [Project2].[CreateDateTime1] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
    [Project2].[IsDeleted1] AS [IsDeleted1]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Limit1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Limit1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        [Limit1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
        [Limit1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
        [Limit1].[C1] AS [C1], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Description] AS [Description], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name1], 
        [Join1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime1], 
        [Join1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted1], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[RoleId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C2]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (1) 
            [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
            [Extent1].[Name] AS [Name], 
            [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], 
            [Extent1].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted], 
            1 AS [C1]
            FROM [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent1]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[RoleId] AS [RoleId], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Description] AS [Description], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent3].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent3].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_RolePermissions] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Permissions] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[PermissionId] ) AS [Join1] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join1].[RoleId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[C2] ASC
